   428	// RegisterAllMetrics registers all prometheus metrics.
   429	func (m *ServerMetrics) RegisterAllMetrics() {
   430	        for _, pm := range m.metrics {
   431	                prometheus.MustRegister(pm)
   432	        }

    40	const (
    41	        // keep the enqueue period a smaller value to make sure the BSL can be validated as expected.
    42	        // The BSL validation frequency is 1 minute by default, if we set the enqueue period as 1 minute,
    43	        // this will cause the actual validation interval for each BSL to be 2 minutes
    44	        bslValidationEnqueuePeriod = 10 * time.Second
    45	)

    47	// BackupStorageLocationReconciler reconciles a BackupStorageLocation object
    48	type backupStorageLocationReconciler struct {
    49	        ctx                       context.Context
    50	        client                    client.Client
    51	        defaultBackupLocationInfo storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo
    52	        // use variables to refer to these functions so they can be
    53	        // replaced with fakes for testing.
    54	        newPluginManager  func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager
    55	        backupStoreGetter persistence.ObjectBackupStoreGetter
    56	
    57	        log logrus.FieldLogger
    58	}
    59	
    60	// NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler initialize and return a backupStorageLocationReconciler struct
    61	func NewBackupStorageLocationReconciler(
    62	        ctx context.Context,
    63	        client client.Client,
    64	        defaultBackupLocationInfo storage.DefaultBackupLocationInfo,
    65	        newPluginManager func(logrus.FieldLogger) clientmgmt.Manager,
    66	        backupStoreGetter persistence.ObjectBackupStoreGetter,
    67	        log logrus.FieldLogger) *backupStorageLocationReconciler {
    68	        return &backupStorageLocationReconciler{
    69	                ctx:                       ctx,
    70	                client:                    client,
    71	                defaultBackupLocationInfo: defaultBackupLocationInfo,
    72	                newPluginManager:          newPluginManager,
    73	                backupStoreGetter:         backupStoreGetter,
    74	                log:                       log,
    75	        }
    76	}
    77	
    78	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=velero.io,resources=backupstoragelocations,verbs=get;list;watch;create;update;patch;delete
    79	// +kubebuilder:rbac:groups=velero.io,resources=backupstoragelocations/status,verbs=get;update;patch
    80	
    81	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) Reconcile(ctx context.Context, req ctrl.Request) (ctrl.Result, error) {
    82	        var unavailableErrors []string
    83	        var location velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
    84	
    85	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).WithField(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation, req.NamespacedName.String())
    86	        log.Debug("Validating availability of BackupStorageLocation")
    87	
    88	        locationList, err := storage.ListBackupStorageLocations(r.ctx, r.client, req.Namespace)
    89	        if err != nil {
    90	                log.WithError(err).Error("No BackupStorageLocations found, at least one is required")
    91	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        pluginManager := r.newPluginManager(log)
    95	        defer pluginManager.CleanupClients()
    96	
    97	        // find the BSL that matches the request
    98	        for _, bsl := range locationList.Items {
    99	                if bsl.Name == req.Name && bsl.Namespace == req.Namespace {
   100	                        location = bsl
   101	                }
   102	        }
   103	
   104	        if location.Name == "" || location.Namespace == "" {
   105	                log.WithError(err).Error("BackupStorageLocation is not found")
   106	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // decide the default BSL
   110	        defaultFound, err := r.ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList)
   111	        if err != nil {
   112	                log.WithError(err).Error("failed to ensure single default bsl")
   113	                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        func() {
   117	                var err error
   118	                original := location.DeepCopy()
   119	                defer func() {
   120	                        location.Status.LastValidationTime = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now().UTC()}
   121	                        if err != nil {
   122	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocation is invalid, marking as unavailable")
   123	                                err = errors.Wrapf(err, "BackupStorageLocation %q is unavailable", location.Name)
   124	                                unavailableErrors = append(unavailableErrors, err.Error())
   125	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable
   126	                                location.Status.Message = err.Error()
   127	                        } else {
   128	                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocations is valid, marking as available")
   129	                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable
   130	                                location.Status.Message = ""
   131	                        }
   132	                        if err := r.client.Patch(r.ctx, &location, client.MergeFrom(original)); err != nil {
   133	                                log.WithError(err).Error("Error updating BackupStorageLocation phase")
   134	                        }
   135	                }()
   136	
   137	                backupStore, err := r.backupStoreGetter.Get(&location, pluginManager, log)
   138	                if err != nil {
   139	                        log.WithError(err).Error("Error getting a backup store")
   140	                        return
   141	                }
   142	
   143	                log.Info("Validating BackupStorageLocation")
   144	                err = backupStore.IsValid()
   145	                if err != nil {
   146	                        log.WithError(err).Error("fail to validate backup store")
   147	                        return
   148	                }
   149	        }()
   150	
   151	        r.logReconciledPhase(defaultFound, locationList, unavailableErrors)
   152	
   153	        return ctrl.Result{}, nil
   154	}
   155	
   156	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) logReconciledPhase(defaultFound bool, locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList, errs []string) {
   157	        var availableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   158	        var unAvailableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   159	        var unknownBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   160	        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation)
   161	
   162	        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
   163	                phase := location.Status.Phase
   164	                switch phase {
   165	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable:
   166	                        availableBSLs = append(availableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   167	                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable:
   168	                        unAvailableBSLs = append(unAvailableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   169	                default:
   170	                        unknownBSLs = append(unknownBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   171	                }
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        numAvailable := len(availableBSLs)
   175	        numUnavailable := len(unAvailableBSLs)
   176	        numUnknown := len(unknownBSLs)
   177	
   178	        if numUnavailable+numUnknown == len(locationList.Items) { // no available BSL
   179	                if len(errs) > 0 {
   180	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   181	                } else {
   182	                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown)
   183	                }
   184	        } else if numUnavailable > 0 { // some but not all BSL unavailable
   185	                log.Warnf("Unavailable BackupStorageLocations detected: available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        if !defaultFound {
   189	                log.Warn("There is no existing BackupStorageLocation set as default. Please see `velero backup-location -h` for options.")
   190	        }
   191	}
   192	
   193	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) SetupWithManager(mgr ctrl.Manager) error {
   194	        gp := kube.NewGenericEventPredicate(func(object client.Object) bool {
   195	                location := object.(*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation)
   196	                return storage.IsReadyToValidate(location.Spec.ValidationFrequency, location.Status.LastValidationTime, r.defaultBackupLocationInfo.ServerValidationFrequency, r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation))
   197	        })
   198	        g := kube.NewPeriodicalEnqueueSource(
   199	                r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation),
   200	                mgr.GetClient(),
   201	                &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{},
   202	                bslValidationEnqueuePeriod,
   203	                kube.PeriodicalEnqueueSourceOption{
   204	                        Predicates: []predicate.Predicate{gp},
   205	                },
   206	        )
   207	
   208	        return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
   209	                // As the "status.LastValidationTime" field is always updated, this triggers new reconciling process, skip the update event that include no spec change to avoid the reconcile loop
   210	                For(&velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}, builder.WithPredicates(kube.SpecChangePredicate{})).
   211	                WatchesRawSource(g).
   212	                Named(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).
   213	                Complete(r)
   214	}
   215	
   216	// ensureSingleDefaultBSL ensures that there is only one default BSL in the namespace.
   217	// the default BSL priority is as follows:
   218	// 1. follow the user's setting (the most recent validation BSL is the default BSL)
   219	// 2. follow the server's setting ("velero server --default-backup-storage-location")
   220	func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList) (bool, error) {
   221	        // get all default BSLs
   222	        var defaultBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   223	        var defaultFound bool
   224	        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
   225	                if location.Spec.Default {
   226	                        defaultBSLs = append(defaultBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
   227	                }
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        if len(defaultBSLs) > 1 { // more than 1 default BSL
   231	                // find the most recent updated default BSL
   232	                var mostRecentCreatedBSL *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
   233	                defaultFound = true
   234	                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
   235	                        if mostRecentCreatedBSL == nil {
   236	                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
   237	                                continue
   238	                        }
   239	                        // For lack of a better way to compare timestamps, we use the CreationTimestamp
   240	                        // it cloud not really find the most recent updated BSL, but it is good enough for now
   241	                        bslTimestamp := bsl.CreationTimestamp
   242	                        mostRecentTimestamp := mostRecentCreatedBSL.CreationTimestamp
   243	                        if mostRecentTimestamp.Before(&bslTimestamp) {
   244	                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
   245	                        }
   246	                }
   247	
   248	                // unset all other default BSLs
   249	                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
   250	                        if bsl.Name != mostRecentCreatedBSL.Name {
   251	                                bsl.Spec.Default = false
   252	                                if err := r.client.Update(r.ctx, bsl); err != nil {
   253	                                        return defaultFound, errors.Wrapf(err, "failed to unset default backup storage location %q", bsl.Name)
   254	                                }
   255	                                r.log.Debugf("update default backup storage location %q to false", bsl.Name)
   256	                        }
   257	                }
   258	        } else if len(defaultBSLs) == 0 { // no default BSL
   259	                defaultFound = false
   260	        } else { // only 1 default BSL
   261	                defaultFound = true
   262	        }
   263	        return defaultFound, nil
   264	}

    90	func NewCommand(f client.Factory) *cobra.Command {
    91	        config := config.GetDefaultConfig()
    92	
    93	        var command = &cobra.Command{
    94	                Use:    "server",
    95	                Short:  "Run the velero server",
    96	                Long:   "Run the velero server",
    97	                Hidden: true,
    98	                Run: func(c *cobra.Command, args []string) {
    99	                        // go-plugin uses log.Println to log when it's waiting for all plugin processes to complete so we need to
   100	                        // set its output to stdout.
   101	                        log.SetOutput(os.Stdout)
   102	
   103	                        logLevel := config.LogLevel.Parse()
   104	                        format := config.LogFormat.Parse()
   105	
   106	                        // Make sure we log to stdout so cloud log dashboards don't show this as an error.
   107	                        logrus.SetOutput(os.Stdout)
   108	
   109	                        // Velero's DefaultLogger logs to stdout, so all is good there.
   110	                        logger := logging.DefaultLogger(logLevel, format)
   111	
   112	                        logger.Infof("setting log-level to %s", strings.ToUpper(logLevel.String()))
   113	
   114	                        logger.Infof("Starting Velero server %s (%s)", buildinfo.Version, buildinfo.FormattedGitSHA())
   115	                        if len(features.All()) > 0 {
   116	                                logger.Infof("%d feature flags enabled %s", len(features.All()), features.All())
   117	                        } else {
   118	                                logger.Info("No feature flags enabled")
   119	                        }
   120	
   121	                        f.SetBasename(fmt.Sprintf("%s-%s", c.Parent().Name(), c.Name()))
   122	
   123	                        s, err := newServer(f, config, logger)
   124	                        cmd.CheckError(err)
   125	
   126	                        cmd.CheckError(s.run())
   127	                },
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        config.BindFlags(command.Flags())
   131	
   132	        return command
   133	}
   134	
   135	type server struct {
   136	        namespace        string
   137	        metricsAddress   string
   138	        kubeClientConfig *rest.Config
   139	        kubeClient       kubernetes.Interface
   140	        discoveryClient  discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryInterface
   141	        discoveryHelper  velerodiscovery.Helper
   142	        dynamicClient    dynamic.Interface
   143	        // controller-runtime client. the difference from the controller-manager's client
   144	        // is that the controller-manager's client is limited to list namespaced-scoped
   145	        // resources in the namespace where Velero is installed, or the cluster-scoped
   146	        // resources. The crClient doesn't have the limitation.
   147	        crClient              ctrlclient.Client
   148	        ctx                   context.Context
   149	        cancelFunc            context.CancelFunc
   150	        logger                logrus.FieldLogger
   151	        logLevel              logrus.Level
   152	        pluginRegistry        process.Registry
   153	        repoManager           repomanager.Manager
   154	        repoLocker            *repository.RepoLocker
   155	        repoEnsurer           *repository.Ensurer
   156	        metrics               *metrics.ServerMetrics
   157	        config                *config.Config
   158	        mgr                   manager.Manager
   159	        credentialFileStore   credentials.FileStore
   160	        credentialSecretStore credentials.SecretStore
   161	}
   162	
   163	func newServer(f client.Factory, config *config.Config, logger *logrus.Logger) (*server, error) {
   164	        if msg, err := uploader.ValidateUploaderType(config.UploaderType); err != nil {
   165	                return nil, err
   166	        } else if msg != "" {
   167	                logger.Warn(msg)
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        if config.ClientQPS < 0.0 {
   171	                return nil, errors.New("client-qps must be positive")
   172	        }
   173	        f.SetClientQPS(config.ClientQPS)
   174	
   175	        if config.ClientBurst <= 0 {
   176	                return nil, errors.New("client-burst must be positive")
   177	        }
   178	        f.SetClientBurst(config.ClientBurst)
   179	
   180	        if config.ClientPageSize < 0 {
   181	                return nil, errors.New("client-page-size must not be negative")
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        kubeClient, err := f.KubeClient()
   185	        if err != nil {
   186	                return nil, err
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        dynamicClient, err := f.DynamicClient()
   190	        if err != nil {
   191	                return nil, err
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        crClient, err := f.KubebuilderClient()
   195	        if err != nil {
   196	                return nil, err
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        pluginRegistry := process.NewRegistry(config.PluginDir, logger, logger.Level)
   200	        if err := pluginRegistry.DiscoverPlugins(); err != nil {
   201	                return nil, err
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        // cancelFunc is not deferred here because if it was, then ctx would immediately
   205	        // be canceled once this function exited, making it useless to any informers using later.
   206	        // That, in turn, causes the velero server to halt when the first informer tries to use it.
   207	        // Therefore, we must explicitly call it on the error paths in this function.
   208	        ctx, cancelFunc := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
   209	
   210	        clientConfig, err := f.ClientConfig()
   211	        if err != nil {
   212	                cancelFunc()
   213	                return nil, err
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
   217	        if err := velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   218	                cancelFunc()
   219	                return nil, err
   220	        }
   221	        if err := velerov2alpha1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   222	                cancelFunc()
   223	                return nil, err
   224	        }
   225	        if err := corev1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   226	                cancelFunc()
   227	                return nil, err
   228	        }
   229	        if err := snapshotv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   230	                cancelFunc()
   231	                return nil, err
   232	        }
   233	        if err := batchv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   234	                cancelFunc()
   235	                return nil, err
   236	        }
   237	        if err := appsv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
   238	                cancelFunc()
   239	                return nil, err
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        ctrl.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger))
   243	        klog.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger)) // klog.Logger is used by k8s.io/client-go
   244	
   245	        var mgr manager.Manager
   246	        retry := 10
   247	        for {
   248	                mgr, err = ctrl.NewManager(clientConfig, ctrl.Options{
   249	                        Scheme: scheme,
   250	                        Cache: cache.Options{
   251	                                DefaultNamespaces: map[string]cache.Config{
   252	                                        f.Namespace(): {},
   253	                                },
   254	                        },
   255	                })
   256	                if err == nil {
   257	                        break
   258	                }
   259	
   260	                retry--
   261	                if retry == 0 {
   262	                        break
   263	                }
   264	
   265	                logger.WithError(err).Warn("Failed to create controller manager, need retry")
   266	
   267	                time.Sleep(time.Second)
   268	        }
   269	
   270	        if err != nil {
   271	                cancelFunc()
   272	                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating controller manager")
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        credentialFileStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedFileStore(
   276	                mgr.GetClient(),
   277	                f.Namespace(),
   278	                config.CredentialsDirectory,
   279	                filesystem.NewFileSystem(),
   280	        )
   281	        if err != nil {
   282	                cancelFunc()
   283	                return nil, err
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        credentialSecretStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedSecretStore(mgr.GetClient(), f.Namespace())
   287	        if err != nil {
   288	                cancelFunc()
   289	                return nil, err
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        var discoveryClient discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryInterface
   293	        if discoveryClient, err = f.DiscoveryClient(); err != nil {
   294	                cancelFunc()
   295	                return nil, err
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        s := &server{
   299	                namespace:             f.Namespace(),
   300	                metricsAddress:        config.MetricsAddress,
   301	                kubeClientConfig:      clientConfig,
   302	                kubeClient:            kubeClient,
   303	                discoveryClient:       discoveryClient,
   304	                dynamicClient:         dynamicClient,
   305	                crClient:              crClient,
   306	                ctx:                   ctx,
   307	                cancelFunc:            cancelFunc,
   308	                logger:                logger,
   309	                logLevel:              logger.Level,
   310	                pluginRegistry:        pluginRegistry,
   311	                config:                config,
   312	                mgr:                   mgr,
   313	                credentialFileStore:   credentialFileStore,
   314	                credentialSecretStore: credentialSecretStore,
   315	        }
   316	
   317	        return s, nil
   318	}
   319	
   320	func (s *server) run() error {
   321	        signals.CancelOnShutdown(s.cancelFunc, s.logger)
   322	
   323	        if s.config.ProfilerAddress != "" {
   324	                go s.runProfiler()
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        // Since s.namespace, which specifies where backups/restores/schedules/etc. should live,
   328	        // *could* be different from the namespace where the Velero server pod runs, check to make
   329	        // sure it exists, and fail fast if it doesn't.
   330	        if err := s.namespaceExists(s.namespace); err != nil {
   331	                return err
   332	        }
   333	
   334	        if err := s.initDiscoveryHelper(); err != nil {
   335	                return err
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        if err := s.veleroResourcesExist(); err != nil {
   339	                return err
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        s.checkNodeAgent()
   343	
   344	        if err := s.initRepoManager(); err != nil {
   345	                return err
   346	        }
   347	
   348	        if err := s.setupBeforeControllerRun(); err != nil {
   349	                return err
   350	        }
   351	
   352	        if err := s.runControllers(s.config.DefaultVolumeSnapshotLocations.Data()); err != nil {
   353	                return err
   354	        }
   355	
   356	        return nil
   357	}
   358	
   359	// setupBeforeControllerRun do any setup that needs to happen before the controllers are started.
   360	func (s *server) setupBeforeControllerRun() error {
   361	        client, err := ctrlclient.New(s.mgr.GetConfig(), ctrlclient.Options{Scheme: s.mgr.GetScheme()})
   362	        // the function is called before starting the controller manager, the embedded client isn't ready to use, so create a new one here
   363	        if err != nil {
   364	                return errors.WithStack(err)
   365	        }
   366	
   367	        markInProgressCRsFailed(s.ctx, client, s.namespace, s.logger)
   368	
   369	        if err := setDefaultBackupLocation(s.ctx, client, s.namespace, s.config.DefaultBackupLocation, s.logger); err != nil {
   370	                return err
   371	        }
   372	        return nil
   373	}
   374	
   375	// setDefaultBackupLocation set the BSL that matches the "velero server --default-backup-storage-location"
   376	func setDefaultBackupLocation(ctx context.Context, client ctrlclient.Client, namespace, defaultBackupLocation string, logger logrus.FieldLogger) error {
   377	        if defaultBackupLocation == "" {
   378	                logger.Debug("No default backup storage location specified. Velero will not automatically select a backup storage location for new backups.")
   379	                return nil
   380	        }
   381	
   382	        backupLocation := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}
   383	        if err := client.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: defaultBackupLocation}, backupLocation); err != nil {
   384	                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
   385	                        logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).WithError(err).Warn("Failed to set default backup storage location at server start")
   386	                        return nil
   387	                } else {
   388	                        return errors.WithStack(err)
   389	                }
   390	        }
   391	
   392	        if !backupLocation.Spec.Default {
   393	                backupLocation.Spec.Default = true
   394	                if err := client.Update(ctx, backupLocation); err != nil {
   395	                        return errors.WithStack(err)
   396	                }
   397	
   398	                logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).Info("Set backup storage location as default")
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        return nil
   402	}
   403	
   404	// namespaceExists returns nil if namespace can be successfully
   405	// gotten from the Kubernetes API, or an error otherwise.
   406	func (s *server) namespaceExists(namespace string) error {
   407	        s.logger.WithField("namespace", namespace).Info("Checking existence of namespace.")
   408	
   409	        if _, err := s.kubeClient.CoreV1().Namespaces().Get(s.ctx, namespace, metav1.GetOptions{}); err != nil {
   410	                return errors.WithStack(err)
   411	        }
   412	
   413	        s.logger.WithField("namespace", namespace).Info("Namespace exists")
   414	        return nil
   415	}
   416	
   417	// initDiscoveryHelper instantiates the server's discovery helper and spawns a
   418	// goroutine to call Refresh() every 5 minutes.
   419	func (s *server) initDiscoveryHelper() error {
   420	        discoveryHelper, err := velerodiscovery.NewHelper(s.discoveryClient, s.logger)
   421	        if err != nil {
   422	                return err
   423	        }
   424	        s.discoveryHelper = discoveryHelper
   425	
   426	        go wait.Until(
   427	                func() {
   428	                        if err := discoveryHelper.Refresh(); err != nil {
   429	                                s.logger.WithError(err).Error("Error refreshing discovery")
   430	                        }
   431	                },
   432	                5*time.Minute,
   433	                s.ctx.Done(),
   434	        )
   435	
   436	        return nil
   437	}
   438	
   439	// veleroResourcesExist checks for the existence of each Velero CRD via discovery
   440	// and returns an error if any of them don't exist.
   441	func (s *server) veleroResourcesExist() error {
   442	        s.logger.Info("Checking existence of Velero custom resource definitions")
   443	
   444	        // add more group versions whenever available
   445	        gvResources := map[string]sets.Set[string]{
   446	                velerov1api.SchemeGroupVersion.String():       velerov1api.CustomResourceKinds(),
   447	                velerov2alpha1api.SchemeGroupVersion.String(): velerov2alpha1api.CustomResourceKinds(),
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        for _, lst := range s.discoveryHelper.Resources() {
   451	                if resources, found := gvResources[lst.GroupVersion]; found {
   452	                        for _, resource := range lst.APIResources {
   453	                                s.logger.WithField("kind", resource.Kind).Info("Found custom resource")
   454	                                resources.Delete(resource.Kind)
   455	                        }
   456	                }
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        var errs []error
   460	        for gv, resources := range gvResources {
   461	                for kind := range resources {
   462	                        errs = append(errs, errors.Errorf("custom resource %s not found in Velero API group %s", kind, gv))
   463	                }
   464	        }
   465	
   466	        if len(errs) > 0 {
   467	                errs = append(errs, errors.New("Velero custom resources not found - apply config/crd/v1/bases/*.yaml,config/crd/v2alpha1/bases*.yaml, to update the custom resource definitions"))
   468	                return kubeerrs.NewAggregate(errs)
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        s.logger.Info("All Velero custom resource definitions exist")
   472	        return nil
   473	}
   474	
   475	func (s *server) checkNodeAgent() {
   476	        // warn if node agent does not exist
   477	        if kube.WithLinuxNode(s.ctx, s.crClient, s.logger) {
   478	                if err := nodeagent.IsRunningOnLinux(s.ctx, s.kubeClient, s.namespace); err == nodeagent.ErrDaemonSetNotFound {
   479	                        s.logger.Warn("Velero node agent not found for linux nodes; pod volume backups/restores and data mover backups/restores will not work until it's created")
   480	                } else if err != nil {
   481	                        s.logger.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Warn("Error checking for existence of velero node agent for linux nodes")
   482	                }
   483	        }
   484	
   485	        if kube.WithWindowsNode(s.ctx, s.crClient, s.logger) {
   486	                if err := nodeagent.IsRunningOnWindows(s.ctx, s.kubeClient, s.namespace); err == nodeagent.ErrDaemonSetNotFound {
   487	                        s.logger.Warn("Velero node agent not found for Windows nodes; pod volume backups/restores and data mover backups/restores will not work until it's created")
   488	                } else if err != nil {
   489	                        s.logger.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Warn("Error checking for existence of velero node agent for Windows nodes")
   490	                }
   491	        }
   492	}
   493

    46	var _ = Describe("Backup Storage Location Reconciler", func() {
    47	        It("Should successfully patch a backup storage location object status phase according to whether its storage is valid or not", func() {
    48	                tests := []struct {
    49	                        backupLocation    *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
    50	                        isValidError      error
    51	                        expectedIsDefault bool
    52	                        expectedPhase     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhase
    53	                }{
    54	                        {
    55	                                backupLocation:    builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-1").ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).Default(true).Result(),
    56	                                isValidError:      nil,
    57	                                expectedIsDefault: true,
    58	                                expectedPhase:     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable,
    59	                        },
    60	                        {
    61	                                backupLocation:    builder.ForBackupStorageLocation("ns-1", "location-2").ValidationFrequency(1 * time.Second).Result(),
    62	                                isValidError:      errors.New("an error"),
    63	                                expectedIsDefault: false,
    64	                                expectedPhase:     velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable,
    65	                        },
    66	                }
    67

+        if config.ClientBurst <= 0 {
+                return nil, errors.New("client-burst must be positive")
+        }
+        f.SetClientBurst(config.ClientBurst)
+
+        if config.ClientPageSize < 0 {
+                return nil, errors.New("client-page-size must not be negative")
+        }
+
+        kubeClient, err := f.KubeClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        dynamicClient, err := f.DynamicClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        crClient, err := f.KubebuilderClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        pluginRegistry := process.NewRegistry(config.PluginDir, logger, logger.Level)
+        if err := pluginRegistry.DiscoverPlugins(); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // cancelFunc is not deferred here because if it was, then ctx would immediately
+        // be canceled once this function exited, making it useless to any informers using later.
+        // That, in turn, causes the velero server to halt when the first informer tries to use it.
+        // Therefore, we must explicitly call it on the error paths in this function.
+        ctx, cancelFunc := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
+
+        clientConfig, err := f.ClientConfig()
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
+        if err := velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := velerov2alpha1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := corev1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := snapshotv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := batchv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := appsv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        ctrl.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger))
+        klog.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger)) // klog.Logger is used by k8s.io/client-go
+
+        var mgr manager.Manager
+        retry := 10
+        for {
+                mgr, err = ctrl.NewManager(clientConfig, ctrl.Options{
+                        Scheme: scheme,
+                        Cache: cache.Options{
+                                DefaultNamespaces: map[string]cache.Config{
+                                        f.Namespace(): {},
+                                },
+                        },
+                })
+                if err == nil {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                retry--
+                if retry == 0 {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                logger.WithError(err).Warn("Failed to create controller manager, need retry")
+
+                time.Sleep(time.Second)
+        }
+
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating controller manager")
+        }
+
+        credentialFileStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedFileStore(
+                mgr.GetClient(),
+                f.Namespace(),
+                config.CredentialsDirectory,
+                filesystem.NewFileSystem(),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        credentialSecretStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedSecretStore(mgr.GetClient(), f.Namespace())
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        var discoveryClient discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryInterface
+        if discoveryClient, err = f.DiscoveryClient(); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        s := &server{
+                namespace:             f.Namespace(),
+                metricsAddress:        config.MetricsAddress,
+                kubeClientConfig:      clientConfig,
+                kubeClient:            kubeClient,
+                discoveryClient:       discoveryClient,
+                dynamicClient:         dynamicClient,
+                crClient:              crClient,
+                ctx:                   ctx,
+                cancelFunc:            cancelFunc,
+                logger:                logger,
+                logLevel:              logger.Level,
+                pluginRegistry:        pluginRegistry,
+                config:                config,
+                mgr:                   mgr,
+                credentialFileStore:   credentialFileStore,
+                credentialSecretStore: credentialSecretStore,
+        }
+
+        return s, nil
 }

 // setDefaultBackupLocation set the BSL that matches the "velero server --default-backup-storage-location"

-			return errors.WithStack(err)
-		}

-		if err := client.Update(ctx, backupLocation); err != nil {

+        if defaultBackupLocation == "" {
+                logger.Debug("No default backup storage location specified. Velero will not automatically select a backup storage location for new backups.")
+                return nil
+        }
+
+        backupLocation := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}
+        if err := client.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: defaultBackupLocation}, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+                        logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).WithError(err).Warn("Failed to set default backup storage location at server start")
+                        return nil
+                } else {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        if !backupLocation.Spec.Default {
+                backupLocation.Spec.Default = true
+                if err := client.Update(ctx, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+
+                logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).Info("Set backup storage location as default")
+        }
+

 }

+        // By far, PodVolumeBackup, PodVolumeRestore, BackupStorageLocation controllers
+        // are not included in --disable-controllers list.
+        // This is because of PVB and PVR are used by node agent DaemonSet,
+        // and BSL controller is mandatory for Velero to work.
+        // Note: all runtime type controllers that can be disabled are grouped separately, below:
+        enabledRuntimeControllers := map[string]struct{}{
+                constant.ControllerBackup:              {},
+                constant.ControllerBackupDeletion:      {},

+                }
+        }
+
+        s.logger.Info("Server starting...")
+
+        if err := s.mgr.Start(s.ctx); err != nil {
+                s.logger.Fatal("Problem starting manager", err)
+        }
+        return nil
 }
 
 // removeControllers will remove any controller listed to be disabled from the list
 // of controllers to be initialized. It will check the runtime controllers. If a match
 // wasn't found and it returns an error.
 func removeControllers(disabledControllers []string, enabledRuntimeControllers map[string]struct{}, logger logrus.FieldLogger) error {
-	for _, controllerName := range disabledControllers {
-		if _, ok := enabledRuntimeControllers[controllerName]; ok {
-			logger.Infof("Disabling controller: %s", controllerName)
-			delete(enabledRuntimeControllers, controllerName)
-		} else {
-			msg := fmt.Sprintf("Invalid value for --disable-controllers flag provided: %s. Valid values are: %s", controllerName, strings.Join(config.DisableableControllers, ","))
-			return errors.New(msg)
-		}
-	}
-	return nil
+        for _, controllerName := range disabledControllers {
+                if _, ok := enabledRuntimeControllers[controllerName]; ok {
+                        logger.Infof("Disabling controller: %s", controllerName)
+                        delete(enabledRuntimeControllers, controllerName)
+                } else {
+                        msg := fmt.Sprintf("Invalid value for --disable-controllers flag provided: %s. Valid values are: %s", controllerName, strings.Join(config.DisableableControllers, ","))
+                        return errors.New(msg)
+                }
+        }
+        return nil
 }

+        mux.HandleFunc("/debug/pprof/", pprof.Index)
+        mux.HandleFunc("/debug/pprof/cmdline", pprof.Cmdline)
+        mux.HandleFunc("/debug/pprof/profile", pprof.Profile)
+        mux.HandleFunc("/debug/pprof/symbol", pprof.Symbol)
+        mux.HandleFunc("/debug/pprof/trace", pprof.Trace)
+
+        server := &http.Server{
+                Addr:              s.config.ProfilerAddress,
+                Handler:           mux,
+                ReadHeaderTimeout: 3 * time.Second,
+        }
+        if err := server.ListenAndServe(); err != nil {
+                s.logger.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Error("error running profiler http server")
+        }
 }
 
 // if there is a restarting during the reconciling of backups/restores/etc, these CRs may be stuck in progress status
 // markInProgressCRsFailed tries to mark the in progress CRs as failed when starting the server to avoid the issue
 func markInProgressCRsFailed(ctx context.Context, client ctrlclient.Client, namespace string, log logrus.FieldLogger) {
-	markInProgressBackupsFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
+        markInProgressBackupsFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
 
-	markInProgressRestoresFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
+        markInProgressRestoresFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
 }

-	}
-
-	for i, backup := range backups.Items {

-			continue
-		}
-		updated := backup.DeepCopy()
-		updated.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupPhaseFailed

+                log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Error("failed to list backups")
+                return
+        }
+
+        for i, backup := range backups.Items {
+                if backup.Status.Phase != velerov1api.BackupPhaseInProgress {
+                        log.Debugf("the status of backup %q is %q, skip", backup.GetName(), backup.Status.Phase)
+                        continue
+                }
+                updated := backup.DeepCopy()
+                updated.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupPhaseFailed
+                updated.Status.FailureReason = fmt.Sprintf("found a backup with status %q during the server starting, mark it as %q", backup.Status.Phase, updated.Status.Phase)
+                updated.Status.CompletionTimestamp = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()}
+                if err := client.Patch(ctx, updated, ctrlclient.MergeFrom(&backups.Items[i])); err != nil {
+                        log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Errorf("failed to patch backup %q", backup.GetName())
+                        continue
+                }
+                log.WithField("backup", backup.GetName()).Warn(updated.Status.FailureReason)
+                markDataUploadsCancel(ctx, client, backup, log)
+                markPodVolumeBackupsCancel(ctx, client, backup, log)
+        }
 }

+        if msg, err := uploader.ValidateUploaderType(config.UploaderType); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        } else if msg != "" {
+                logger.Warn(msg)
+        }
+
+        if config.ClientQPS < 0.0 {
+                return nil, errors.New("client-qps must be positive")
+        }
+        f.SetClientQPS(config.ClientQPS)
+
+        if config.ClientBurst <= 0 {
+                return nil, errors.New("client-burst must be positive")
+        }
+        f.SetClientBurst(config.ClientBurst)
+
+        if config.ClientPageSize < 0 {
+                return nil, errors.New("client-page-size must not be negative")
+        }
+
+        kubeClient, err := f.KubeClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        dynamicClient, err := f.DynamicClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        crClient, err := f.KubebuilderClient()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        pluginRegistry := process.NewRegistry(config.PluginDir, logger, logger.Level)
+        if err := pluginRegistry.DiscoverPlugins(); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // cancelFunc is not deferred here because if it was, then ctx would immediately
+        // be canceled once this function exited, making it useless to any informers using later.
+        // That, in turn, causes the velero server to halt when the first informer tries to use it.
+        // Therefore, we must explicitly call it on the error paths in this function.
+        ctx, cancelFunc := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
+
+        clientConfig, err := f.ClientConfig()
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
+        if err := velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := velerov2alpha1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := corev1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := snapshotv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := batchv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := appsv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        ctrl.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger))
+        klog.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger)) // klog.Logger is used by k8s.io/client-go
+
+        var mgr manager.Manager
+        retry := 10
+        for {
+                mgr, err = ctrl.NewManager(clientConfig, ctrl.Options{
+                        Scheme: scheme,
+                        Cache: cache.Options{
+                                DefaultNamespaces: map[string]cache.Config{
+                                        f.Namespace(): {},
+                                },
+                        },
+                })
+                if err == nil {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                retry--
+                if retry == 0 {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                logger.WithError(err).Warn("Failed to create controller manager, need retry")
+
+                time.Sleep(time.Second)
+        }
+
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating controller manager")
+        }
+
+        credentialFileStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedFileStore(
+                mgr.GetClient(),
+                f.Namespace(),
+                config.CredentialsDirectory,
+                filesystem.NewFileSystem(),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        credentialSecretStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedSecretStore(mgr.GetClient(), f.Namespace())
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        var discoveryClient discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryInterface
+        if discoveryClient, err = f.DiscoveryClient(); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        s := &server{
+                namespace:             f.Namespace(),
+                metricsAddress:        config.MetricsAddress,
+                kubeClientConfig:      clientConfig,
+                kubeClient:            kubeClient,
+                discoveryClient:       discoveryClient,
+                dynamicClient:         dynamicClient,
+                crClient:              crClient,
+                ctx:                   ctx,
+                cancelFunc:            cancelFunc,
+                logger:                logger,
+                logLevel:              logger.Level,
+                pluginRegistry:        pluginRegistry,
+                config:                config,
+                mgr:                   mgr,
+                credentialFileStore:   credentialFileStore,
+                credentialSecretStore: credentialSecretStore,
+        }
+
+        return s, nil
 }

+        if defaultBackupLocation == "" {
+                logger.Debug("No default backup storage location specified. Velero will not automatically select a backup storage location for new backups.")
+                return nil
+        }
+
+        backupLocation := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}
+        if err := client.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: defaultBackupLocation}, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+                        logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).WithError(err).Warn("Failed to set default backup storage location at server start")
+                        return nil
+                } else {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        if !backupLocation.Spec.Default {
+                backupLocation.Spec.Default = true
+                if err := client.Update(ctx, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+
+                logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).Info("Set backup storage location as default")
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }

+        s.logger.Info("Server starting...")
+
+        if err := s.mgr.Start(s.ctx); err != nil {
+                s.logger.Fatal("Problem starting manager", err)
+        }
+        return nil
 }
 
 // removeControllers will remove any controller listed to be disabled from the list
 // of controllers to be initialized. It will check the runtime controllers. If a match
 // wasn't found and it returns an error.
 func removeControllers(disabledControllers []string, enabledRuntimeControllers map[string]struct{}, logger logrus.FieldLogger) error {
-	for _, controllerName := range disabledControllers {
-		if _, ok := enabledRuntimeControllers[controllerName]; ok {
-			logger.Infof("Disabling controller: %s", controllerName)
-			delete(enabledRuntimeControllers, controllerName)
-		} else {
-			msg := fmt.Sprintf("Invalid value for --disable-controllers flag provided: %s. Valid values are: %s", controllerName, strings.Join(config.DisableableControllers, ","))
-			return errors.New(msg)
-		}
-	}
-	return nil
+        for _, controllerName := range disabledControllers {
+                if _, ok := enabledRuntimeControllers[controllerName]; ok {
+                        logger.Infof("Disabling controller: %s", controllerName)
+                        delete(enabledRuntimeControllers, controllerName)
+                } else {
+                        msg := fmt.Sprintf("Invalid value for --disable-controllers flag provided: %s. Valid values are: %s", controllerName, strings.Join(config.DisableableControllers, ","))
+                        return errors.New(msg)
+                }
+        }
+        return nil
 }

 // if there is a restarting during the reconciling of backups/restores/etc, these CRs may be stuck in progress status
 // markInProgressCRsFailed tries to mark the in progress CRs as failed when starting the server to avoid the issue
 func markInProgressCRsFailed(ctx context.Context, client ctrlclient.Client, namespace string, log logrus.FieldLogger) {
-	markInProgressBackupsFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
+        markInProgressBackupsFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
 
-	markInProgressRestoresFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
+        markInProgressRestoresFailed(ctx, client, namespace, log)
 }

-	if err := client.List(ctx, backups, &ctrlclient.ListOptions{Namespace: namespace}); err != nil {
-		log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Error("failed to list backups")
-		return
-	}
-
-	for i, backup := range backups.Items {
-		if backup.Status.Phase != velerov1api.BackupPhaseInProgress {
-			log.Debugf("the status of backup %q is %q, skip", backup.GetName(), backup.Status.Phase)
-			continue
-		}
-		updated := backup.DeepCopy()
-		updated.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupPhaseFailed
-		updated.Status.FailureReason = fmt.Sprintf("found a backup with status %q during the server starting, mark it as %q", backup.Status.Phase, updated.Status.Phase)
-		updated.Status.CompletionTimestamp = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()}
-		if err := client.Patch(ctx, updated, ctrlclient.MergeFrom(&backups.Items[i])); err != nil {
-			log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Errorf("failed to patch backup %q", backup.GetName())

-		}
-		log.WithField("backup", backup.GetName()).Warn(updated.Status.FailureReason)

+        backups := &velerov1api.BackupList{}
+        if err := client.List(ctx, backups, &ctrlclient.ListOptions{Namespace: namespace}); err != nil {
+                log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Error("failed to list backups")
+                return
+        }
+
+        for i, backup := range backups.Items {
+                if backup.Status.Phase != velerov1api.BackupPhaseInProgress {
+                        log.Debugf("the status of backup %q is %q, skip", backup.GetName(), backup.Status.Phase)
+                        continue
+                }
+                updated := backup.DeepCopy()
+                updated.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupPhaseFailed
+                updated.Status.FailureReason = fmt.Sprintf("found a backup with status %q during the server starting, mark it as %q", backup.Status.Phase, updated.Status.Phase)
+                updated.Status.CompletionTimestamp = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now()}
+                if err := client.Patch(ctx, updated, ctrlclient.MergeFrom(&backups.Items[i])); err != nil {
+                        log.WithError(errors.WithStack(err)).Errorf("failed to patch backup %q", backup.GetName())
+                        continue
+                }
+                log.WithField("backup", backup.GetName()).Warn(updated.Status.FailureReason)
+                markDataUploadsCancel(ctx, client, backup, log)
+                markPodVolumeBackupsCancel(ctx, client, backup, log)
+        }
 }

+        var unavailableErrors []string
+        var location velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+
+        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).WithField(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation, req.NamespacedName.String())
+        log.Debug("Validating availability of BackupStorageLocation")
+
+        locationList, err := storage.ListBackupStorageLocations(r.ctx, r.client, req.Namespace)
+        if err != nil {
+                log.WithError(err).Error("No BackupStorageLocations found, at least one is required")
+                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        pluginManager := r.newPluginManager(log)
+        defer pluginManager.CleanupClients()
+
+        // find the BSL that matches the request
+        for _, bsl := range locationList.Items {
+                if bsl.Name == req.Name && bsl.Namespace == req.Namespace {
+                        location = bsl
+                }
+        }
+
+        if location.Name == "" || location.Namespace == "" {
+                log.WithError(err).Error("BackupStorageLocation is not found")
+                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        // decide the default BSL
+        defaultFound, err := r.ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList)
+        if err != nil {
+                log.WithError(err).Error("failed to ensure single default bsl")
+                return ctrl.Result{}, nil
+        }
+
+        func() {
+                var err error
+                original := location.DeepCopy()
+                defer func() {
+                        location.Status.LastValidationTime = &metav1.Time{Time: time.Now().UTC()}
+                        if err != nil {
+                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocation is invalid, marking as unavailable")
+                                err = errors.Wrapf(err, "BackupStorageLocation %q is unavailable", location.Name)
+                                unavailableErrors = append(unavailableErrors, err.Error())
+                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable
+                                location.Status.Message = err.Error()
+                                r.metrics.RegisterBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(location.Name, metrics.BackupLastStatusFailure)
+                        } else {
+                                log.Info("BackupStorageLocations is valid, marking as available")
+                                location.Status.Phase = velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable
+                                location.Status.Message = ""
+                                r.metrics.RegisterBackupStorageLocationLastStatus(location.Name, metrics.BackupLastStatusSucc)
+                        }
+                        if err := r.client.Patch(r.ctx, &location, client.MergeFrom(original)); err != nil {
+                                log.WithError(err).Error("Error updating BackupStorageLocation phase")
+                        }
+                }()
+
+                backupStore, err := r.backupStoreGetter.Get(&location, pluginManager, log)
+                if err != nil {
+                        log.WithError(err).Error("Error getting a backup store")
+                        return
+                }
+
+                log.Info("Validating BackupStorageLocation")
+                err = backupStore.IsValid()
+                if err != nil {
+                        log.WithError(err).Error("fail to validate backup store")
+                        return
+                }
+        }()
+
+        r.logReconciledPhase(defaultFound, locationList, unavailableErrors)
+
+        return ctrl.Result{}, nil
 }
 
 func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) logReconciledPhase(defaultFound bool, locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList, errs []string) {

-		switch phase {

-			availableBSLs = append(availableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
-		case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable:
-			unAvailableBSLs = append(unAvailableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
-		default:
-			unknownBSLs = append(unknownBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
-		}
-	}
-
-	numAvailable := len(availableBSLs)
-	numUnavailable := len(unAvailableBSLs)
-	numUnknown := len(unknownBSLs)
-
-	if numUnavailable+numUnknown == len(locationList.Items) { // no available BSL
-		if len(errs) > 0 {
-			log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
-		} else {
-			log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown)
-		}
-	} else if numUnavailable > 0 { // some but not all BSL unavailable
-		log.Warnf("Unavailable BackupStorageLocations detected: available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
-	}
-

-		log.Warn("There is no existing BackupStorageLocation set as default. Please see `velero backup-location -h` for options.")
-	}
+        var availableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+        var unAvailableBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+        var unknownBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+        log := r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation)
+
+        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
+                phase := location.Status.Phase
+                switch phase {
+                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseAvailable:
+                        availableBSLs = append(availableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
+                case velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationPhaseUnavailable:
+                        unAvailableBSLs = append(unAvailableBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
+                default:
+                        unknownBSLs = append(unknownBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
+                }
+        }
+
+        numAvailable := len(availableBSLs)
+        numUnavailable := len(unAvailableBSLs)
+        numUnknown := len(unknownBSLs)
+
+        if numUnavailable+numUnknown == len(locationList.Items) { // no available BSL
+                if len(errs) > 0 {
+                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
+                } else {
+                        log.Errorf("Current BackupStorageLocations available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown)
+                }
+        } else if numUnavailable > 0 { // some but not all BSL unavailable
+                log.Warnf("Unavailable BackupStorageLocations detected: available/unavailable/unknown: %v/%v/%v, %s)", numAvailable, numUnavailable, numUnknown, strings.Join(errs, "; "))
+        }
+
+        if !defaultFound {
+                log.Warn("There is no existing BackupStorageLocation set as default. Please see `velero backup-location -h` for options.")
+        }
 }

-		// As the "status.LastValidationTime" field is always updated, this triggers new reconciling process, skip the update event that include no spec change to avoid the reconcile loop

+        gp := kube.NewGenericEventPredicate(func(object client.Object) bool {
+                location := object.(*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation)
+                return storage.IsReadyToValidate(location.Spec.ValidationFrequency, location.Status.LastValidationTime, r.defaultBackupLocationInfo.ServerValidationFrequency, r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation))
+        })
+        g := kube.NewPeriodicalEnqueueSource(
+                r.log.WithField("controller", constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation),
+                mgr.GetClient(),
+                &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList{},
+                bslValidationEnqueuePeriod,
+                kube.PeriodicalEnqueueSourceOption{
+                        Predicates: []predicate.Predicate{gp},
+                },
+        )
+
+        return ctrl.NewControllerManagedBy(mgr).
+                // As the "status.LastValidationTime" field is always updated, this triggers new reconciling process, skip the update event that include no spec change to avoid the reconcile loop
+                For(&velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}, builder.WithPredicates(kube.SpecChangePredicate{})).
+                WatchesRawSource(g).
+                Named(constant.ControllerBackupStorageLocation).
+                Complete(r)
 }
 
 // ensureSingleDefaultBSL ensures that there is only one default BSL in the namespace.

 // 1. follow the user's setting (the most recent validation BSL is the default BSL)
 // 2. follow the server's setting ("velero server --default-backup-storage-location")
 func (r *backupStorageLocationReconciler) ensureSingleDefaultBSL(locationList velerov1api.BackupStorageLocationList) (bool, error) {
-	// get all default BSLs
-	var defaultBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
-	var defaultFound bool
-	for i, location := range locationList.Items {
-		if location.Spec.Default {

-		}
-	}
-
-	if len(defaultBSLs) > 1 { // more than 1 default BSL
-		// find the most recent updated default BSL
-		var mostRecentCreatedBSL *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
-		defaultFound = true
-		for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
-			if mostRecentCreatedBSL == nil {
-				mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
-				continue
-			}
-			// For lack of a better way to compare timestamps, we use the CreationTimestamp
-			// it cloud not really find the most recent updated BSL, but it is good enough for now
-			bslTimestamp := bsl.CreationTimestamp
-			mostRecentTimestamp := mostRecentCreatedBSL.CreationTimestamp
-			if mostRecentTimestamp.Before(&bslTimestamp) {
-				mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
-			}
-		}
-
-		// unset all other default BSLs
-		for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
-			if bsl.Name != mostRecentCreatedBSL.Name {
-				bsl.Spec.Default = false
-				if err := r.client.Update(r.ctx, bsl); err != nil {
-					return defaultFound, errors.Wrapf(err, "failed to unset default backup storage location %q", bsl.Name)
-				}
-				r.log.Debugf("update default backup storage location %q to false", bsl.Name)
-			}
-		}
-	} else if len(defaultBSLs) == 0 { // no default BSL
-		defaultFound = false
-	} else { // only 1 default BSL
-		defaultFound = true
-	}
-	return defaultFound, nil
+        // get all default BSLs
+        var defaultBSLs []*velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+        var defaultFound bool
+        for i, location := range locationList.Items {
+                if location.Spec.Default {
+                        defaultBSLs = append(defaultBSLs, &locationList.Items[i])
+                }
+        }
+
+        if len(defaultBSLs) > 1 { // more than 1 default BSL
+                // find the most recent updated default BSL
+                var mostRecentCreatedBSL *velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation
+                defaultFound = true
+                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
+                        if mostRecentCreatedBSL == nil {
+                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
+                                continue
+                        }
+                        // For lack of a better way to compare timestamps, we use the CreationTimestamp
+                        // it cloud not really find the most recent updated BSL, but it is good enough for now
+                        bslTimestamp := bsl.CreationTimestamp
+                        mostRecentTimestamp := mostRecentCreatedBSL.CreationTimestamp
+                        if mostRecentTimestamp.Before(&bslTimestamp) {
+                                mostRecentCreatedBSL = bsl
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // unset all other default BSLs
+                for _, bsl := range defaultBSLs {
+                        if bsl.Name != mostRecentCreatedBSL.Name {
+                                bsl.Spec.Default = false
+                                if err := r.client.Update(r.ctx, bsl); err != nil {
+                                        return defaultFound, errors.Wrapf(err, "failed to unset default backup storage location %q", bsl.Name)
+                                }
+                                r.log.Debugf("update default backup storage location %q to false", bsl.Name)
+                        }
+                }
+        } else if len(defaultBSLs) == 0 { // no default BSL
+                defaultFound = false
+        } else { // only 1 default BSL
+                defaultFound = true
+        }
+        return defaultFound, nil
 }

+                        ),
+                        DataDownloadFailureTotal: prometheus.NewCounterVec(
+                                prometheus.CounterOpts{
+                                        Namespace: podVolumeMetricsNamespace,
+                                        Name:      DataDownloadFailureTotal,
+                                        Help:      "Total number of failed downloaded snapshots",
+                                },
+                                []string{nodeMetricLabel},
+                        ),
+                        DataDownloadCancelTotal: prometheus.NewCounterVec(
+                                prometheus.CounterOpts{
+                                        Namespace: podVolumeMetricsNamespace,
+                                        Name:      DataDownloadCancelTotal,
+                                        Help:      "Total number of canceled downloaded snapshots",
+                                },
+                                []string{nodeMetricLabel},
+                        ),
+                },
+        }
 }

+        pluginRegistry := process.NewRegistry(config.PluginDir, logger, logger.Level)
+        if err := pluginRegistry.DiscoverPlugins(); err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // cancelFunc is not deferred here because if it was, then ctx would immediately
+        // be canceled once this function exited, making it useless to any informers using later.
+        // That, in turn, causes the velero server to halt when the first informer tries to use it.
+        // Therefore, we must explicitly call it on the error paths in this function.
+        ctx, cancelFunc := context.WithCancel(context.Background())
+
+        clientConfig, err := f.ClientConfig()
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
+        if err := velerov1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := velerov2alpha1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := corev1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := snapshotv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := batchv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        if err := appsv1api.AddToScheme(scheme); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        ctrl.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger))
+        klog.SetLogger(logrusr.New(logger)) // klog.Logger is used by k8s.io/client-go
+
+        var mgr manager.Manager
+        retry := 10
+        for {
+                mgr, err = ctrl.NewManager(clientConfig, ctrl.Options{
+                        Scheme: scheme,
+                        Cache: cache.Options{
+                                DefaultNamespaces: map[string]cache.Config{
+                                        f.Namespace(): {},
+                                },
+                        },
+                })
+                if err == nil {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                retry--
+                if retry == 0 {
+                        break
+                }
+
+                logger.WithError(err).Warn("Failed to create controller manager, need retry")
+
+                time.Sleep(time.Second)
+        }
+
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, errors.Wrap(err, "error creating controller manager")
+        }
+
+        credentialFileStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedFileStore(
+                mgr.GetClient(),
+                f.Namespace(),
+                config.CredentialsDirectory,
+                filesystem.NewFileSystem(),
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        credentialSecretStore, err := credentials.NewNamespacedSecretStore(mgr.GetClient(), f.Namespace())
+        if err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        var discoveryClient discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryInterface
+        if discoveryClient, err = f.DiscoveryClient(); err != nil {
+                cancelFunc()
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        s := &server{
+                namespace:             f.Namespace(),
+                metricsAddress:        config.MetricsAddress,
+                kubeClientConfig:      clientConfig,
+                kubeClient:            kubeClient,
+                discoveryClient:       discoveryClient,
+                dynamicClient:         dynamicClient,
+                crClient:              crClient,
+                ctx:                   ctx,
+                cancelFunc:            cancelFunc,
+                logger:                logger,
+                logLevel:              logger.Level,
+                pluginRegistry:        pluginRegistry,
+                config:                config,
+                mgr:                   mgr,
+                credentialFileStore:   credentialFileStore,
+                credentialSecretStore: credentialSecretStore,
+        }
+
+        return s, nil
 }

-			return errors.WithStack(err)

+        if defaultBackupLocation == "" {
+                logger.Debug("No default backup storage location specified. Velero will not automatically select a backup storage location for new backups.")
+                return nil
+        }
+
+        backupLocation := &velerov1api.BackupStorageLocation{}
+        if err := client.Get(ctx, types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: defaultBackupLocation}, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                if apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+                        logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).WithError(err).Warn("Failed to set default backup storage location at server start")
+                        return nil
+                } else {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+        }
+
+        if !backupLocation.Spec.Default {
+                backupLocation.Spec.Default = true
+                if err := client.Update(ctx, backupLocation); err != nil {
+                        return errors.WithStack(err)
+                }
+
+                logger.WithField("backupStorageLocation", defaultBackupLocation).Info("Set backup storage location as default")
+        }
+
+        return nil
 }

+                velerov1api.SchemeGroupVersion.String():       velerov1api.CustomResourceKinds(),
+                velerov2alpha1api.SchemeGroupVersion.String(): velerov2alpha1api.CustomResourceKinds(),

+
